Every\n   190→\t// element of queue should be in the dirty set and not in the\n   191→\t// processing set.\n   192→\tqueue Queue[t]\n   193→\n   194→\t// dirty defines all of the items that need to be processed.\n   195→\tdirty set[t]\n   196→\n   197→\t// Things that are currently being processed are in the processing set.\n   198→\t// These things may be simultaneously in the dirty set. The functions below are always\n// called from the same goroutine.\ntype Queue[T comparable] interface {\n\t// Touch can be hooked when an existing item is added again. This may be\n\t// useful if the implementation allows priority change for the given item.\n\tTouch(item T)\n\t// Push adds a new item.\n\tPush(item T)\n\t// Len tells the total number of items.\n\tLen() int\n\t// Pop retrieves an item.\n\tPop() (item T)\n}\n\n// DefaultQueue is a slice based FIFO queue.\nfunc DefaultQueue[T comparable]() Queue[T] {\n\treturn new(queue[T])\n}\n\n// queue is a slice which implements Queue.\ntype queue[T comparable] []T\n\nfunc (q *queue[T]) Touch(item T) {}\n\nfunc (q *queue[T]) Push(item T) {\n\t*q = append(*q, item)\n}\n\nfunc (q *queue[T]) Len() int {\n\treturn len(*q)\n}\n\nfunc (q *queue[T]) Pop() (item T) {\n\titem = (*q)[0]\n\n\t// The underlying array still exists and reference this object, so the object will not be garbage collected.\n\t(*q)[0] = *new(T)\n\t*q = (*q)[1:]\n\n\treturn item\n}\n\n// QueueConfig specifies optional configurations to customize an Interface.\n// Deprecated: use TypedQueueConfig instead.\ntype QueueConfig = TypedQueueConfig[any]\n\ntype TypedQueueConfig[T comparable] struct {\n\t// Name for the queue. If unnamed, the metrics will not be registered.\n\tName string\n\n\t// MetricsProvider optionally allows specifying a metrics provider to use for the queue\n\t// instead of the global provider.\n\tMetricsProvider MetricsProvider\n\n\t// Clock ability to inject real or fake clock for testing purposes.\n\tClock clock.WithTicker\n\n\t// Queue provides the underlying queue to use. &Typed[T]{\n\t\tclock:                      c,\n\t\tqueue:                      queue,\n\t\tdirty:                      set[T]{},\n\t\tprocessing:                 set[T]{},\n\t\tcond: time.Millisecond\n\n// Type is a work queue (see the package comment).\n// Deprecated: Use Typed instead.\ntype Type = Typed[any]\n\ntype Typed[t comparable] struct {\n\t// queue defines the order in which we will work on items. Every\n\t// element of queue should be in the dirty set and not in the\n\t// processing set.\n\tqueue Queue[t]\n\n\t// dirty defines all of the items that need to be processed.\n\tdirty set[t]\n\n\t// Things that are currently being processed are in the processing set.\n\t// These things may be simultaneously in the dirty set. When we finish\n\t// processing something and remove it from this set, we'll check if\n\t// it's in the dirty set, and if so, add it to the queue.\n\tprocessing set[t]\n\n\tcond *sync.Cond\n\n\tshuttingDown bool\n\tdrain        bool\n\n\tmetrics queueMetrics[t]\n\n\tunfinishedWorkUpdatePeriod time.Duration\n\tclock                      clock.WithTicker\n}\n\ntype empty struct{}\ntype set[t comparable] map[t]empty\n\nfunc (s set[t]) has(item t) bool {\n\t_, exists := s[item]\n\treturn exists\n}\n\nfunc (s set[t]) insert(item t) {\n\ts[item] = empty{}\n}\n\nfunc (s set[t]) delete(item t) {\n\tdelete(s, item)\n}\n\nfunc (s set[t]) len() int {\n\treturn len(s)\n}\n\n// Add marks item as needing processing.\nfunc (q *Typed[T]) Add(item T) {\n\tq.cond.L.Lock()\n\tdefer q.cond.L.Unlock()\n\tif q.shuttingDown {\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\tif q.dirty.has(item) {\n\t\t// the same item is added again before it is processed, call the Touch\n\t\t// function if the queue cares about it (for e.g, reset its priority)\n\t\tif !q.processing.has(item) {\n\t\t\tq.queue.Touch(item)\n\t\t}\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\n\tq.metrics.add(item)\n\n\tq.dirty.insert(item)\n\tif q.processing.has(item) {\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\n\tq.queue.Push(item)\n\tq.cond.Signal()\n}\n\n// Len returns the current queue length, for informational purposes only. You\n// shouldn't e.g. gate a call to Add() or Get() on Len() being a particular\n// value, that can't be synchronized properly.\nfunc (q *Typed[T]) Len() int {\n\tq.cond.L.Lock()\n\tdefer q.cond.L.Unlock()\n\treturn q.queue.Len()\n}\n\n// Get blocks until it can return an item to be processed. If shutdown = true,\n// the caller should end their goroutine. You must call Done with item when you\n// have finished processing it.\nfunc (q *Typed[T]) Get() (item T, shutdown bool) {\n\tq.cond.L.Lock()\n\tdefer q.cond.L.Unlock()\n\tfor q.queue.Len() == 0 && !q.shuttingDown {\n\t\tq.cond.Wait()\n\t}\n\tif q.queue.Len() == 0 {\n\t\t// We must be shutting down.\n\t\treturn *new(T), true\n\t}\n\n\titem = q.queue.Pop()\n\n\tq.metrics.get(item)\n\n\tq.processing.insert(item)\n\tq.dirty.delete(item)\n\n\treturn item, false\n}\n\n// Done marks item as done processing, and if it has been marked as dirty again\n// while it was being processed, it will be re-added to the queue for\n// re-processing.\nfunc (q *Typed[T]) Done(item T) {\n\tq.cond.L.Lock()\n\tdefer q.cond.L.Unlock()\n\n\tq.metrics.done(item)\n\n\tq.processing.delete(item)\n\tif q.dirty.has(item) {\n\t\tq.queue.Push(item)\n\t\tq.cond.Signal()\n\t} else if q.processing.len() == 0 {\n\t\tq.cond.Signal()\n\t}\n}\n\n// ShutDown will cause q to ignore all new items added to it and\n// immediately instruct the worker goroutines to exit.\nfunc (q *Typed[T]) ShutDown() {\n\tq.cond.L.Lock()\n\tdefer q.cond.L.Unlock()\n\n\tq.drain = false\n\tq.shuttingDown = true\n\tq.cond.Broadcast()\n}\n\n// ShutDownWithDrain will cause q to ignore all new items added to it. As soon\n// as the worker goroutines have \"drained\", i.e: finished processing and called\n// Done on all existing items in the queue; they will be instructed to exit and\n// ShutDownWithDrain will return. Hence: a strict requirement for using this is;\n// your workers must ensure that Done is called on all items in the queue once\n// the shut down has been initiated, if that is not the case: this will block\n// indefinitely. It is, however, safe to call ShutDown after having called\n// ShutDownWithDrain, as to force the queue shut down to terminate immediately\n// without waiting for the drainage.\nfunc (q *Typed[T]) ShutDownWithDrain() {\n\tq.cond.L.Lock()\n\tdefer q.cond.L.Unlock()\n\n\tq.drain = true\n\tq.shuttingDown = true\n\tq.cond.Broadcast()\n\n\tfor q.processing.len() != 0 && q.drain {\n\t\tq.cond.Wait()\n\t}\n}\n\nfunc (q *Typed[T]) ShuttingDown() bool {\n\tq.cond.L.Lock()\n\tdefer q.cond.L.Unlock()\n\n\treturn q.shuttingDown\n}\n\nfunc (q *Typed[T]) updateUnfinishedWorkLoop() {\n\tt := q.clock.NewTicker(q.unfinishedWorkUpdatePeriod)\n\tdefer t.Stop()\n\tfor range t.C() {\n\t\tif !func() bool {\n\t\t\tq.cond.L.Lock()\n\t\t\tdefer q.cond.L.Unlock()\n\t\t\tif !q.shuttingDown {\n\t\t\t\tq.metrics.updateUnfinishedWork()\n\t\t\t\treturn true\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\treturn false\n\n\t\t}() {\n\t\t\treturn\n\t\t}\n\t}\n}\n","numLines":370,"startLine":1,"totalLines":370}}}

183→//\n   184→// waitForPriorityQueue implements heap.Interface. The item occurring next in\n   185→// time (i.e., the item with the smallest readyAt) is at the root (index 0).\n   186→// Peek returns this minimum item at index 0. \"kubernetes/kubernetes\",\n      \"path\": \"staging/src/k8s.io/client-go/examples/workqueue/main.go\",\n      \"symbol\": \"runWorker\"\n    }\n  ],\n  \"text\": \"The Kubernetes controller work queue with rate limiting is implemented primarily in the client-go library, which is vendored into the kubernetes/kubernetes repository under staging/src/k8s.io/client-go/.\\n\\n## Core Workqueue Implementation\\n\\nThe workqueue system consists of multiple layers:\\n\\n1. **Base Queue Interface** (staging/src/k8s.io/client-go/util/workqueue/queue.go):\\n   - Defines TypedInterface with Add(), Get(), Done(), Len(), ShutDown() methods\\n   - Implements Typed[T] struct with FIFO queue behavior\\n   - Manages dirty and processing sets to prevent duplicate concurrent processing\\n\\n2. **Delaying Queue** (staging/src/k8s.io/client-go/util/workqueue/delaying_queue.go):\\n   - Implements TypedDelayingInterface extending TypedInterface\\n   - Adds AddAfter() method for delayed item processing\\n   - Uses priority queue (heap) to manage items scheduled for future addition\\n   - Wraps base Typed queue with delay capabilities\\n\\n3. **Rate Limiting Queue** (staging/src/k8s.io/client-go/util/workqueue/rate_limiting_queue.go):\\n   - Implements TypedRateLimitingInterface extending TypedDelayingInterface\\n   - Adds AddRateLimited(), Forget(), NumRequeues() methods\\n   - Integrates rate limiters to control item requeue timing\\n\\n## Rate Limiter Implementations\\n\\nThe default_rate_limiters.go file defines multiple rate limiter types:\\n\\n1. **TypedRateLimiter Interface**: Base interface with When(), Forget(), NumRequeues() methods\\n\\n2. **TypedBucketRateLimiter** (BucketRateLimiter): Token bucket implementation using golang.org/x/time/rate.Limiter for overall system rate limiting\\n\\n3. **TypedItemExponentialFailureRateLimiter** (ItemExponentialFailureRateLimiter): Implements exponential backoff per item (baseDelay * 2^failures) with configurable max delay\\n\\n4. **TypedItemFastSlowRateLimiter**: Per-item rate limiter with fast retries for N attempts, then slower retries\\n\\n5. **TypedMaxOfRateLimiter**: Composite limiter returning maximum delay from multiple limiters\\n\\n6. **TypedWithMaxWaitRateLimiter**: Wrapper limiting maximum wait time regardless of underlying limiter\\n\\n7. **DefaultTypedControllerRateLimiter**: Combines ItemExponentialFailureRateLimiter and BucketRateLimiter via MaxOfRateLimiter\\n\\n## Controller Reconcile Loop Pattern\\n\\nThe reconcile loop using Add/Get/Done pattern appears in:\\n\\n1. **staging/src/k8s.io/sample-controller/controller.go**:\\n   - Creates TypedRateLimitingInterface[cache.ObjectName] queue\\n   - runWorker() continuously calls processNextWorkItem()\\n   - processNextWorkItem() implements the pattern:\\n     - Get() retrieves item and shutdown flag\\n     - defer Done() ensures cleanup\\n     - syncHandler() performs business logic\\n     - AddRateLimited() on error for retry with backoff\\n     - Forget() on success to clear retry history\\n\\n2. **staging/src/k8s.io/client-go/examples/workqueue/main.go**:\\n   - Demonstrates basic controller pattern with TypedRateLimitingInterface[string]\\n   - Shows complete flow: queue creation, informer integration, worker loop\\n   - processNextItem() and runWorker() implement standard reconcile pattern\\n   - handleErr() manages retry logic with NumRequeues() limit\\n\\nThe pattern is universal across all Kubernetes controllers: items are added to queue via informer event handlers, workers process items with Get/Done/AddRateLimited pattern, and rate limiting prevents resource exhaustion while providing exponential backoff for failures.\"\n}\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}

Doc comments are already written\n// as if the code was there.\n\n// MockQueue is an implementation of [TypedRateLimitingInterface] which\n// can be used to test a function which pulls work items out of a queue\n// and processes them. It is thread-safe.\n//\n// A null instance is directly usable. The usual usage is:\n//\n//\tvar m workqueue.Mock[string]\n//\tm.SyncOne(\"some-item\", func(queue workqueue.TypedRateLimitingInterface[string]) { ... } )\n//\tif diff := cmp.Diff(workqueue.MockState[string]{}, m.State()); diff != \"\" {\n//\t    t.Errorf(\"unexpected state of mock work queue after sync (-want, +got):\\n%s\", diff)\n//\t}\n//\n// All slices get reset to nil when they become empty, so there are no spurious\n// differences because of nil vs. empty slice.\ntype Mock[T comparable] struct {\n\tmutex sync.Mutex\n\tstate MockState[T]\n}\n\ntype MockState[T comparable] struct {\n\t// Ready contains the items which are ready for processing.\n\tReady []T\n\n\t// InFlight contains the items which are currently being processed (= Get\n\t// was called, Done not yet).\n\tInFlight []T\n\n\t// MismatchedDone contains the items for which Done was called without\n\t// a matching Get.\n\tMismatchedDone []T\n\n\t// Later contains the items which are meant to be added to the queue after\n\t// a certain delay (= AddAfter was called for them). They appear in the\n\t// order in which AddAfter got called.\n\tLater []MockDelayedItem[T]\n\n\t// Failures contains the items and their retry count which failed to be\n\t// processed (AddRateLimited called at least once, Forget not yet).\n\t// The retry count is always larger than zero.\n\tFailures map[T]int\n\n\t// ShutDownCalled tracks how often ShutDown got called.\n\tShutDownCalled int\n\n\t// ShutDownWithDrainCalled tracks how often ShutDownWithDrain got called.\n\tShutDownWithDrainCalled int\n}\n\n// DeepCopy takes a snapshot of all slices. It cannot do a deep copy of the items in those slices,\n// but typically those keys are immutable.\nfunc (m MockState[T]) DeepCopy() *MockState[T] {\n\tm.Ready = slices.Clone(m.Ready)\n\tm.InFlight = slices.Clone(m.InFlight)\n\tm.MismatchedDone = slices.Clone(m.MismatchedDone)\n\tm.Later = slices.Clone(m.Later)\n\tm.Failures = maps.Clone(m.Failures)\n\treturn &m\n}\n\n// MockDelayedItem is an item which was queue for later processing.\ntype MockDelayedItem[T comparable] struct {\n\tItem     T\n\tDuration time.Duration\n}\n\n// SyncOne adds the item to the work queue and calls sync.\n// That sync function can pull one or more items from the work\n// queue until the queue is empty. Then it is told that the queue\n// is shutting down, which must cause it to return.\n//\n// The test can then retrieve the state of the queue to check the result.\nfunc (m *Mock[T]) SyncOne(item T, sync func(workqueue.TypedRateLimitingInterface[T])) {\n\t// sync must run with the mutex not locked.\n\tdefer sync(m)\n\tm.mutex.Lock()\n\tdefer m.mutex.Unlock()\n\n\tm.state.Ready = append(m.state.Ready, item)\n}\n\n// State returns the current state of the queue.\nfunc (m *Mock[T]) State() MockState[T] {\n\tm.mutex.Lock()\n\tdefer m.mutex.Unlock()\n\n\treturn *m.state.DeepCopy()\n}\n\n// Add implements [TypedInterface].\nfunc (m *Mock[T]) Add(item T) {\n\tm.mutex.Lock()\n\tdefer m.mutex.Unlock()\n\n\tif !slices.Contains(m.state.Ready, item) {\n\t\tm.state.Ready = append(m.state.Ready, item)\n\t}\n}\n\n// Len implements [TypedInterface].\nfunc (m *Mock[T]) Len() int {\n\tm.mutex.Lock()\n\tdefer m.mutex.Unlock()\n\n\treturn len(m.state.Ready)\n}\n\n// Get implements [TypedInterface].\nfunc (m *Mock[T]) Get() (item T, shutdown bool) {\n\tm.mutex.Lock()\n\tdefer m.mutex.Unlock()\n\n\tif len(m.state.Ready) == 0 {\n\t\tshutdown = true\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\titem = m.state.Ready[0]\n\tm.state.Ready = m.state.Ready[1:]\n\tif len(m.state.Ready) == 0 {\n\t\tm.state.Ready = nil\n\t}\n\tm.state.InFlight = append(m.state.InFlight, item)\n\treturn item, false\n}\n\n// Done implements [TypedInterface].\nfunc (m *Mock[T]) Done(item T) {\n\tm.mutex.Lock()\n\tdefer m.mutex.Unlock()\n\n\tindex := slices.Index(m.state.InFlight, item)\n\tif index < 0 {\n\t\tm.state.MismatchedDone = append(m.state.MismatchedDone, item)\n\t}\n\tm.state.InFlight = slices.Delete(m.state.InFlight, index, index+1)\n\tif len(m.state.InFlight) == 0 {\n\t\tm.state.InFlight = nil\n\t}\n}\n\n// ShutDown implements [TypedInterface].\nfunc (m *Mock[T]) ShutDown() {\n\tm.mutex.Lock()\n\tdefer m.mutex.Unlock()\n\n\tm.state.ShutDownCalled++\n}\n\n// ShutDownWithDrain implements [TypedInterface].\nfunc (m *Mock[T]) ShutDownWithDrain() {\n\tm.mutex.Lock()\n\tdefer m.mutex.Unlock()\n\n\tm.state.ShutDownWithDrainCalled++\n}\n\n// ShuttingDown implements [TypedInterface].\nfunc (m *Mock[T]) ShuttingDown() bool {\n\tm.mutex.Lock()\n\tdefer m.mutex.Unlock()\n\n\treturn m.state.ShutDownCalled > 0 || m.state.ShutDownWithDrainCalled > 0\n}\n\n// AddAfter implements [TypedDelayingInterface.AddAfter]\nfunc (m *Mock[T]) AddAfter(item T, duration time.Duration) {\n\tif duration == 0 {\n\t\tm.Add(item)\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\n\tm.mutex.Lock()\n\tdefer m.mutex.Unlock()\n\n\tfor i := range m.state.Later {\n\t\tif m.state.Later[i].Item == item {\n\t\t\t// https://github.com/kubernetes/client-go/blob/270e5ab1714527c455865953da8ceba2810dbb50/util/workqueue/delaying_queue.go#L340-L349\n\t\t\t// only shortens the delay for an existing item. It does not make it longer.\n\t\t\tif m.state.Later[i].Duration > duration {\n\t\t\t\tm.state.Later[i].Duration = duration\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\treturn\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\tm.state.Later = append(m.state.Later, MockDelayedItem[T]{Item: item, Duration: duration})\n}\n\n// AddRateLimited implements [TypedRateLimitingInterface.AddRateLimited].\nfunc (m *Mock[T]) AddRateLimited(item T) {\n\tm.mutex.Lock()\n\tdefer m.mutex.Unlock()\n\n\tif m.state.Failures == nil {\n\t\tm.state.Failures = make(map[T]int)\n\t}\n\tm.state.Failures[item]++\n}\n\n// Forget implements [TypedRateLimitingInterface.Forget].\nfunc (m *Mock[T]) Forget(item T) {\n\tm.mutex.Lock()\n\tdefer m.mutex.Unlock()\n\n\tif m.state.Failures == nil {\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\tdelete(m.state.Failures, item)\n}\n\n// NumRequeues implements [TypedRateLimitingInterface.NumRequeues].\nfunc (m *Mock[T]) NumRequeues(item T) int {\n\tm.mutex.Lock()\n\tdefer m.mutex.Unlock()\n\n\treturn m.state.Failures[item]\n}\n","numLines":248,"startLine":1,"totalLines":248}}}

queue with rate limiting is implemented primarily in the client-go library, which is vendored into the kubernetes/kubernetes repository under staging/src/k8s.io/client-go/.\\n\\n## Core Workqueue Implementation\\n\\nThe workqueue system consists of multiple layers:\\n\\n1. **Base Queue Interface** (staging/src/k8s.io/client-go/util/workqueue/queue.go):\\n   - Defines TypedInterface with Add(), Get(), Done(), Len(), ShutDown() methods\\n   - Implements Typed[T] struct with FIFO queue behavior\\n   - Manages dirty and processing sets to prevent duplicate concurrent processing\\n\\n2. **Delaying Queue** (staging/src/k8s.io/client-go/util/workqueue/delaying_queue.go):\\n   - Implements TypedDelayingInterface extending TypedInterface\\n   - Adds AddAfter() method for delayed item processing\\n   - Uses priority queue (heap) to manage items scheduled for future addition\\n   - Wraps base Typed queue with delay capabilities\\n\\n3. **Rate Limiting Queue** (staging/src/k8s.io/client-go/util/workqueue/rate_limiting_queue.go):\\n   - Implements TypedRateLimitingInterface extending TypedDelayingInterface\\n   - Adds AddRateLimited(), Forget(), NumRequeues() methods\\n   - Integrates rate limiters to control item requeue timing\\n\\n## Rate Limiter Implementations\\n\\nThe default_rate_limiters.go file defines multiple rate limiter types:\\n\\n1. **TypedRateLimiter Interface**: Base interface with When(), Forget(), NumRequeues() methods\\n\\n2. **TypedBucketRateLimiter** (BucketRateLimiter): Token bucket implementation using golang.org/x/time/rate.Limiter for overall system rate limiting\\n\\n3. **TypedItemExponentialFailureRateLimiter** (ItemExponentialFailureRateLimiter): Implements exponential backoff per item (baseDelay * 2^failures) with configurable max delay\\n\\n4. **TypedItemFastSlowRateLimiter**: Per-item rate limiter with fast retries for N attempts, then slower retries\\n\\n5. **TypedMaxOfRateLimiter**: Composite limiter returning maximum delay from multiple limiters\\n\\n6. **TypedWithMaxWaitRateLimiter**: Wrapper limiting maximum wait time regardless of underlying limiter\\n\\n7. **DefaultTypedControllerRateLimiter**: Combines ItemExponentialFailureRateLimiter and BucketRateLimiter via MaxOfRateLimiter\\n\\n## Controller Reconcile Loop Pattern\\n\\nThe reconcile loop using Add/Get/Done pattern appears in:\\n\\n1. **staging/src/k8s.io/sample-controller/controller.go**:\\n   - Creates TypedRateLimitingInterface[cache.ObjectName] queue\\n   - Get(), Done(), Len(), ShutDown() methods\\n   - Implements Typed[T] struct with FIFO queue behavior\\n   - Manages dirty and processing sets to prevent duplicate concurrent processing\\n\\n2. processing\\n   - Uses priority queue (heap) to manage items scheduled for future addition\\n   - Wraps base Typed queue with delay capabilities\\n\\n3. **Rate Limiting Queue** golang.org/x/time/rate.Limiter for overall system rate limiting\\n\\n3. **TypedItemExponentialFailureRateLimiter** (ItemExponentialFailureRateLimiter): Implements exponential backoff per item (baseDelay * 2^failures) with configurable max delay\\n\\n4. **TypedItemFastSlowRateLimiter**: Per-item rate limiter with fast retries for N attempts, then slower retries\\n\\n5. limiter\\n\\n7. **DefaultTypedControllerRateLimiter**: Combines ItemExponentialFailureRateLimiter and BucketRateLimiter via MaxOfRateLimiter\\n\\n## Controller Reconcile Loop Pattern\\n\\nThe
